            THE COMBINED TRANSMISSION DATA OF HARWELL (EXFOR WORK 2218400800009 
            22184005 AND 22184006) AND ORNL (LARSON ET AL.,       2218400800010 
            ORNL/TM-5614, 1976) OVER THE NEUTRON ENERGY RANGE 1 - 2218400800011 
            480 KEV. RADIATION WIDTHS COULD NOT BE DETERMINED FROM2218400800012 
            THE PRESENT DATA AND REMAINED FIXED AT THE VALUES IN  2218400800013 
            BNL325. REFIT DOES NOT AT PRESENT INCLUDE THE CALCULA-2218400800014 
            TION OF INELASTIC SCATTERING IN THE CROSS SECTION     2218400800015 
            ROUTINE, THUS THE DATA ABOVE 480 KEV COULD NOT BE     2218400800016 
            FULLY ANALYSED. ABOVE THIS INELASTIC THRESHOLD IT WAS 2218400800017 
            ASSUMED THERE WERE NO INTERFERENCE TERMS IN THE       2218400800018 
            INELASTIC CROSS SECTION AND THAT THERE WAS NO CORREL- 2218400800019 
            ATION BETWEEN THE ELASTIC AND INELASTIC WIDTHS. THE   2218400800020 
            QUOTED RESONANCE PARAMETERS REPRODUCE THE TOTAL CROSS 2218400800021 
            SECTION FROM 480 - 550 KEV; ABOVE THIS THE PARAMETERS 2218400800022 
            DO NOT REPRODUCE THE OBSERVED CROSS SECTION.          2218400800023
